<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drumstick.html>drumstick</a> (57668)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:drumstick.html>drumstick</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drumstick.html>drumstick</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drumsticks.html>drumsticks</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drumstick.html>drumstickje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:drumstick.html>drumstick</a></span>, the lower <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> of a fowl (especially a chicken).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:drumstick.html>drumstick</a></span>, a stick used for drumming.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:duchten.html>duchten</a> (83804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:duchten.html>duchten</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dochten.html>dochten</a></i>; further etymology uncertain. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. <p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duchten.html>duchten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fear</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>While most forms of the verb are archaic in standard Dutch, the past participle <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geducht.html>geducht</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> on a life of its own and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still commonly used.
</p>

***duelleren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:duelleren.html>duelleren</a> (30596)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">duellō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duelleren.html>duelleren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fight an armed <a href = vnd.unilang:duel.html>duel</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be engaged in an unarmed (usually verbal, e.g. business <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> or legal) confrontation between two parties</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:duelleren.html>duelleren</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">inergatief</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> tweegevecht <a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:duellist.html>duellist</a> (65339)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***duiden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:duiden.html>duiden</a> (15834)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dieden</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">duden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thiuden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þiudijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duiden.html>duiden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to point to, refer to, suggest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:duid.html>Duid</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> ten <a href = vnd.unilang:kwade.html>kwade</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> take it amiss of <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to explain, clarify
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:droom.html>droom</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:duiden.html>duiden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">To explain a dream.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***duiker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:duiker.html>duiker</a> (11884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duiken.html>duiken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duiker.html>duiker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duikers.html>duikers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duiker.html>duikertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/SmallCulvert.jpg/220px-SmallCulvert.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="275" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/SmallCulvert.jpg/330px-SmallCulvert.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/SmallCulvert.jpg/440px-SmallCulvert.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="1250" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A small culvert.</div></div></div>
<ol><li>an underwater diver</li>
<li>a gymnastic diver</li>
<li>a fairly narrow water passage under roads and dikes; a culvert</li>
<li>a type of waterbird; a <a href = vnd.unilang:loon.html>loon</a> (N-Am) or diver (UK)</li>
<li>a type of <a href = vnd.unilang:antilope.html>antilope</a>; a <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:duiker.html>duiker</a></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">an underwater diver</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kikvorsman.html>kikvorsman</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a gymnastic diver</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schoonspringer</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a culvert</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">grondzijl</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlaat.html>verlaat</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">zinker</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a <a href = vnd.unilang:loon.html>loon</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">zeeduiker</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:duim.html>duim</a> (4500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dume</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thūmo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þūmô</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:tomme.html>tomme</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Dumen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Daumen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thumb</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:tomme.html>tomme</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">tumme</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duim.html>duim</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duimen.html>duimen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duimpje.html>duimpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">thumb</span>, the inner-most finger</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">inch</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pintle</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">jointed pivot of a hinge, consisting of the pin and the non-moving leaf</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***duimen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:duimen.html>duimen</a> (8496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duim.html>duim</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duimen.html>duimen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put one or both thumbs up, notably as a gesture of approval or when hitchhiking to ask for a ride</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to twiddle one's thumbs</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep one's <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a> crossed <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">i.e. to show support</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suck on one's thumb</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">duusternesse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thiusternussi</i>. ***duit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:duit.html>duit</a> (26262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:duit.html>duit</a></i>, of uncertain origin. Possibly borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">þveit</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cut-off piece of metal, small coin, <span class="Latn" lang="en">doit</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þwītan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut, cutt off</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (when dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thwite</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duit.html>duit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duiten.html>duiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duit.html>duitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A Dutch copper coin with the value of <small><sup>1</sup><big>⁄</big><sub>160</sub></small> of a <a href = vnd.unilang:guilder.html>guilder</a>, current before the decimalization of 1816.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in the singular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An amount of money, a sum of money.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarmee.html>daarmee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardige.html>aardige</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:duit.html>duit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdienen.html>verdienen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She could make a pretty <b><a href = vnd.unilang:penny.html>penny</a></b> from that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Money in general.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">"<a href = vnd.unilang:blijf.html>Blijf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gore.html>gore</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klauwen.html>klauwen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:duiten.html>duiten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a>," krijste <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrek.html>vrek</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">"Keep your filthy mitts of <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b>moola</b>," the miser shrieked.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:numismatiek.html>numismatiek</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> Nederlandse <a href = vnd.unilang:munt.html>munt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> vóór <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> begin <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:negentiende.html>negentiende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> honderdzestigste <a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gulden.html>gulden</a>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:duvel.html>duvel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">diuval</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">diabolus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">διάβολος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">diábolos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duizend.html>duizend</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thousand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poot.html>poot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the late 18th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duizendpoot.html>duizendpoot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duizendpoten.html>duizendpoten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duizendpoot.html>duizendpootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A centipede, animal of the class Chilopoda.
<ul><li><b>2011</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>Dick</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laan.html>Laan</a>, <i>Pinkeltje <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> flonkersteen</i>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>Over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bospad.html>bospad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lange.html>lange</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rij.html>rij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:duizendpoten.html>duizendpoten</a></b> aanstappen.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A long line of <b>centipedes</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> treading <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the forest path.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A person of many talents, especially one good at multi-tasking; a <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> of all trades.
<ul><li><b>2014</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kuiper.html>Kuiper</a>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:luna.html>Luna</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fortuna.html>Fortuna</a>", in <a href = vnd.unilang:andrea.html>Andrea</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Leerdam amp; Orlanda S. H. Lie amp; Martine Meuwese amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:maria.html>Maria</a> Patijn (eds.), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kennis.html>Kennis</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:beeld.html>beeld</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>Denken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:middeleeuwen.html>Middeleeuwen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeverij.html>Uitgeverij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verloren.html>Verloren</a> page 48.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedenker.html>bedenker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allegorische.html>allegorische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:personage.html>personage</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Romein Boëthius (ca. 480-525), <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:intellectuele.html>intellectuele</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:duizendpoot.html>duizendpoot</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:invloedrijke.html>invloedrijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scharnieren.html>scharnieren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> laat-antieke Romeinse <a href = vnd.unilang:rijk.html>Rijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Latijnse <a href = vnd.unilang:middeleeuwen.html>Middeleeuwen</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The inventor of this allegorical character <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the Roman Boethius (ca. 480-525), an intellectual <b><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> of many talents</b> and one of the most influential pivots between the late-antique Roman Empire and the Latin Middle Ages.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***dumpling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dumpling.html>dumpling</a> (83779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A folk word <span class="defdate">[c. 1600s]</span>, apparently from a Norfolk dialect, of uncertain origin. Perhaps from some <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> word or from dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dump</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="defdate">[late 1800s]</span>,  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ling</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dumpling.html>dumpling</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dumplings.html>dumplings</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A ball of dough that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> cooked and may have a filling and/or additional ingredients in the dough. <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span>
<ol><li>By restriction, a food composed of a dough wrapper around a filling.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">familiar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A term of <a href = vnd.unilang:endearment.html>endearment</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">My little <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dumpling.html>dumpling</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mildly vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of excrement.
<ul><li><b>2018</b> Brent Butt as Brent Herbert Leroy, "<a href = vnd.unilang:sasquatch.html>Sasquatch</a> Your Language", <i>Corner Gas Animated</i>
<dl><dd>Wherever legitimate <a href = vnd.unilang:tracks.html>tracks</a> are found there's always some fresh scat, y'know, poo, flop, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dumplings.html>dumplings</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***dun.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dun.html>dun</a> (5097)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunne.html>dunne</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thunni</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*þunnī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þunnuz</i>. Cognates with English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thin</i> (Compare West-Flemish thinne).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dun.html>dun</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunner.html>dunner</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">dunst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thin, slender</li>
<li>sparse</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">liquid</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> runny</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

***dunken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dunken.html>dunken</a> (30594)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunken.html>dunken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thunken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þunkijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunken.html>dunken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to think, to consider</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunken.html>Dunken</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> one of a few Dutch verbs where the <i>object</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the one having an opinion about something, and the <i>subject</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the thing it <a href = vnd.unilang:concerns.html>concerns</a>. For example, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dunkt.html>dunkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i> means 'I think/consider it good'. For this reason it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally used impersonally.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The past tense forms are archaic and rarely used.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunk.html>dunk</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dunken.html>dunken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> basketball</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:dunk.html>dunk</a></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr />
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
